This is Sayani, 21 years-old, 3rd year, MIT. 

*I got molested at EDGE by the bouncer who's supposed to PROTECT us.*

It's 2 AM at night and I'm typing this 'cause I had to tell this to every student (girls esp) who go out at night, *thinking it's safe in Manipal*. Like a normal Friday, we went outside to party at *EDGE* (all of my friends are from MAHE and legally old enough to party). There was this random guy from SOC (mostly), who was trying to hit on me and my friend asked him to back out. We were a group of 8, both of them got into a fight but were successfully taken apart by our friends. 

Five minutes after, *everything was normal till the bouncer and a localite came to interfere*, mostly 'cause of the girl (Kiran-SOC, 3rd year), the guy's friend, who might have called the bouncer.

They dragged my guy friends out, hurt them, so bad that *one of them is in KMC trauma right now, getting diagnosed if he got his hand fractured*. He has cut marks on his neck which speaks about how badly he was pulled out.

I've often been to Edge, which newly got popular among students, after it changed it's name from Tito's to what it is called now. *Social media, they say, helped it gain it's popularity, and tonight I'm seeking social media to see if it gets me justice for what happened to me*. 

So, 5 minutes after the incident was sorted, the bouncer was hitting my friend, we were trying to stop the bouncer but he didn't just stop, he instead hit me and my other 2 girl friends as well, leave apart guys. I was trying to talk and narrate them what the actual incident was but they hit me back; *that was not the end*, *not once, not twice, not thrice, the bouncer and the localite guy, touched my breasts, squeezed them, and did every possible thing to just feel my private parts in the name of hitting or putting me aside*.

I knew the *manager (Rathan)*, told him about the incident, he came outside acting like he is going to help, but all that he had to say was, *"I'm trying to help you and I'm on your side but I know the bouncer, he is my 'brother', he can't do this"*. 

There was this other shopkeeper who owns a shop under Janani Lodge and maybe he is related to Edge too, he came out to sort the matter and spoke to me but all that he had to say was that *"please don't create a scene, we'll sort it out, but please don't shout, the cops will come"*.
 
*That is all that I wanted, the cops to come*. I wanted to go to the police station but my 'sensible' friends stopped me 'cause they wanted me to do everything with the help of the administration. With all faith in it, I called a friend of mine who is a part of *student support centre*, and then later the president spoke to me.

Tomorrow, I'll go to talk to the Director, I don't know what actions will be taken. There are so many things happening in and around the campus, don't know how these will stop but I really want students to know where they are going and where they think they are actually safe.

It's 2.43 AM, I'm still typing and re-reading and re-correcting this message, my friend is still undergoing his X-Ray at KMC and got 3 pain-killer injections. 

A bouncer who is supposed to protect us and help us, was someone who hit us, molested me, hit me and came on me once he was asked to apologize, despite being told that we'll call the cops. They just told, "you call the cops, we will call ten such cops".

*How unsafe are we students here?* It's not something we're unaware of that students go out to party in Manipal, but what happened to me tonight, I wouldn't want any girl to face that. I'll try my best to shut down Edge.

I recollect crying to the manager about the incident, but all that he had to say was, *"we are with you but we're sure our bouncer didn't do anything"*.

No matter what a girl is, sober/high, *she can still identify what a wrong and what a right touch is*. And there were witnesses too, to the incident. 

I don't know how any of you will help me through it, but I had to share this so that you guys don't go through what I went through tonight.

*I was mad, I was angry, I was helpless, I was crying but I knew what I wanted, I wanted to shut down a place which is not responsible for it's staff, which is not SAFE for us.* 

*I used to think Manipal is the safest place I can ever be, but I'm so sorry to myself for thinking so*.

I'm sure if there weren't others interfering, they would have made sure I ended up with at least a few broken bones and majorly, a broken dignity.

All I plead to you is to share this, *SPAM this* and make sure no one ever goes through this again. PLEASE.

*#ShutDownEdge*
*#MakeManipalSafeForStudents*

😜Tokyo, Japan
 A man was walking past a young girl, when a jagged edge of his briefcase accidentally tore her mini skirt.

Then she took out a pin, put the skirt back together and left.

😜New York, USA

😜London, England

“Do you mind taking me home, sir? I live not far away.”
The Englishman took his jacket off, put it on her, called a cab and took her home safely.

😜Paris, France

😜Sydney, Australia

As per the directives of Government of Karnataka, as a precautionary measure to prevent spreading of COVID-19, MAHE hereby declare holiday for the students of its constituent colleges / institutes in Manipal, Mangalore and Bangalore campuses for a period of one week, from 14th March to 20th March 2020.

 

However, the holidays will not be applicable to;

*   interns and postgraduate students of medical colleges

*   interns and postgraduate students of allied health programs (except Health Information Management).

 

University examinations will be conducted as scheduled.

 

Students are strictly advised to avoid public / social gatherings and travel as a precautionary measure.

27/12/20, 11:26 - Surjith R: Sir,

We are PG students studying under the DOS , MIT.As everyone would agree, the online medium hasn't been very effective as it was very foreign to both students and the faculty.  And with the all the difficulties of the lockdown, everyone has been struggling to keep up, as we were also short on resources. The reopening itself has been a problem for most of us, with all the logistics being so tedious,  and some of us have been travelling long distances just to attend labs. We do understand that the exams have to be held, but you will have to agree that the test would be rendered pointless if we are being tested under such a stressful situation, with so little under our control. Many of us struggle with mental health, and the pandemic hasn't been very kind either. 

We approached the Department of Science, requesting them to extend the exams or increase the gaps between exams but to no avail. Hence we are writing this email as a final plea. Please co-ordinate with the students so that we can have some sort of harmony in the interests of the students, faculty and college management.

Please do not make this to be a case of students trying to find a way around exams, because it is not. We chose the DOS because we wanted the best education we could get, and we do understand that testing is an integral part of it. We are just asking for a choice (online/offline  as the btech studentshave been offered), or longer breaks in between/ before the exams. We just want time to be prepared.

Faithfully,
